5.1 计算大肠杆菌基因组的GC含量

import os
print(os.getcwd())
print(os.listdir("data"))
/MPATHB/ct/ipython/notebook
['.history', 'bak', 'all_species.json', 'ENCFF289HGQ.tsv', 'codon_table.txt', 'Ecoli.fa', 'ehbio.xls', 'ENCFF060LPA.tsv', 'ENCFF262OBL.tsv', 'gencode.gene.bed12', 'ensm.id', 'ENCFF673KYR.tsv', 'gencode.gene.gtf', 'gencode.v24.ENS2SYN', 'GRCh38.idmap', 'GSM1172883_MCF10F.txt', 'GSM1172884_MCF12A.txt', 'GSM1172905_T47DKBluc.txt', 'GSM1172906_UACC812.txt', 'GSM1172907_UACC893.txt', 'GSM1172908_ZR751.txt', 'GSM1172909_ZR7530.txt', 'GSM1172910_ZR75B.txt', 'human_TP53_cDNA.fasta', 'human_TP53_mRNA.fa', 'merge.py', 'meta.tsv', 'reads.fastq', 'reads_id_list.txt', 'rna_part.gbk', 'selected_id_list.txt', 'selected_reads.fa', 'selected_sequences.fa', 'seqs.fa']
fin = open("data/Ecoli.fa", "rt")
seq_length = 0
gc_count = 0
for line in fin:
    # print(line)
    if line[0] == ">":
        continue
    # 注意层级关系
    gc_count = gc_count + line.count("G") + line.count("C")
    seq_length += len(line.strip())
gc_percent = gc_count / seq_length
print("The GC content of E.coli genome is %.2f%%." % (gc_percent * 100))
print("The GC content of E.coli genome is", round(gc_percent * 100, 2), "%")
fin.close()
The GC content of E.coli genome is 55.69%.
The GC content of E.coli genome is 55.69 %

5.2 把人的P53的cDNA序列转录为RNA，再翻译为蛋白质

结果：https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/CCDS/CcdsBrowse.cgi?REQUEST=CCDS&GO=MainBrowse&DATA=CCDS11118.1

fin = open("data/human_TP53_cDNA.fasta", "rt")
tp53_cdna = ""
tp53_mrna = ""
tp53_protein = ""
# 读入序列
for line in fin:
    if line[0] == ">":
        continue
    tp53_cdna = tp53_cdna + line.strip()
#----------------------------
print("TP53 cDNA sequence (Length: ", len(tp53_cdna), "): ", 
      tp53_cdna, sep="")
# 这个地方没有进行反向互补操作，是因为序列数据库中存储的基因序列实际为基因转录的mRNA序列
# 只是做了T,U的替换
tp53_mrna = tp53_cdna.replace("T", "U")
print("TP53 mRNA sequence (Length: ", len(tp53_mrna), "): ", 
      tp53_mrna, sep="")
codon_dict = {}
f_codon = open("data/codon_table.txt", "rt")
for line in f_codon:
    sp = line.strip().split("\t")
    codon = sp[0].replace("T", "U")
    aa = sp[1]
    codon_dict[codon] = aa
for i in range(0, len(tp53_mrna), 3):
    aa = codon_dict[tp53_mrna[i:i + 3]]
    if aa == "Stop":
        break
    tp53_protein += aa
print("TP53 protein sequence (Length: ", len(
    tp53_protein), "): ", tp53_protein, sep="")
fin.close()
f_codon.close()

5.3 作业：求取文件seqs.fa中多条序列的反向互补序列

reverseD = {"A":"T","G":"C","C":"G","T":"A"}
seqL = []
for line in open("data/seqs.fa"):
    if line[0] == ">":
        if seqL:
            seq = ''.join(seqL)
            seqL = list(seq)
            seqL.reverse()
            seq = ''.join(seqL)
            seqL = []
            for nt in seq:
                seqL.append(reverseD[nt])
            print(key)
            print(''.join(seqL))
            seqL = []
        key = line.strip()
    #---------END if---------------------
    else:
        seqL.append(line.strip())
#------------END for (end reading file)------------
# --为什么需要写这一句-------
seq = ''.join(seqL)
seqL = list(seq)
seqL.reverse()
seq = ''.join(seqL)
seqL = []
for nt in seq:
    seqL.append(reverseD[nt])
print(key)
print(''.join(seqL))

fin = open("data/seqs.fa", "rt")
fout1 = open("data/seqs_reverse_1.fa", "wt")
for line in fin:
    if line[0] == ">" or line.strip() == "":
        fout1.write(line)
        continue
    line_reverse = ""
    for i in range(len(line.strip())):
        if line[i] == "A":
            line_reverse += "T"
        elif line[i] == "T":
            line_reverse += "A"
        elif line[i] == "C":
            line_reverse += "G"
        elif line[i] == "G":
            line_reverse += "C"
    fout1.write(line_reverse + "\n")
fin.close()
fout1.close()

5.4 列出大肠杆菌基因组中限制性内切酶SecI的切割位置

SecI识别CCNNGG

import re
fin = open("data/Ecoli.fa", "rt")
ecoli_seq = ""
for line in fin:
    if line[0] == ">":
        continue
    ecoli_seq += line.strip()
positions = [m.start() for m in re.finditer(r"CC[TCAG][TCAG]GG", ecoli_seq)]
print(positions)
fin.close()
[174, 299, 556]

5.5 作业：找出TP53 mRNA序列中的ORF

正链，非嵌套，非重合，没有长度限制。

此答案是个不完美的方法，特别是在ORF重合时，只能找到第一条ORF序列，可能会漏掉更长的ORF序列。

参考：https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/orffinder/

# 关于这个代码的解释请参阅20180121_02_CT_Python_training-chinese2.ipynb
fin = open("data/human_TP53_mRNA.fa", "rt")
tp53_mrna = ""
for line in fin:
    if line[0] == ">":
        continue
    tp53_mrna += line.strip()
orfs = [orf.group(1) for orf in re.finditer(
    r"(ATG([TCAG]{3})*?)(TAA|TGA|TAG)", tp53_mrna, re.I)]
print(orfs)
fin.close()

5.6 FASTA文件处理

  • 读取seqs.fa
  • 计算seqs.fa中序列的数目
  • 在seqs.fa中提取ID为selected_id_list.txt中ID的序列，存入selected_sequences.fa文件
  • 对seqs.fa中的序列按长度从小到大排序，写入seqs_sorted.fa文件
  • 将seqs.fa中的核酸序列转为单行，存入seqs_single_line.fa文件
  • 将seqs.fa中的核酸序列转为多行，每行长度固定为80个字符，存为seqs_multi_line.fa文件

关于这部分请参阅20180121_02_CT_Python_training-chinese2.ipynb

fin=open("data/seqs.fa", "rt")
fin_file_list=fin.readlines()
fin.close()

# 将文件内容以ID号为键，索引在字典seqs_dict中
seqs_dict={}
i=0
while i<len(fin_file_list):
    if fin_file_list[i][0]==">":
        sp=fin_file_list[i].split(" ")
        seq_id=sp[0][1:]
        annotation=fin_file_list[i].strip()
        sequence=""
        j=i+1
        while j<len(fin_file_list) and fin_file_list[j][0]!=">":
            sequence += fin_file_list[j].strip()
            j=j+1
        if not seq_id in seqs_dict:
            seqs_dict[seq_id]=[annotation, sequence]
        i=j
    else:
        i=i+1

# 计算seqs.fa中序列的数目
sequence_count=len(seqs_dict)
print("There are ", sequence_count, " sequences in the FASTA file.", sep="")

# 根据selected_id_list.txt提取序列，写入selected_sequences.fa文件
f_id_list=open("data/selected_id_list.txt", "rt")
f_selected_seqs=open("data/selected_sequences.fa", "wt")
for line in f_id_list:
    f_selected_seqs.write(seqs_dict[line.strip()][0]+"\n"+seqs_dict[line.strip()][1]+"\n")
f_id_list.close()
f_selected_seqs.close()

# 对seqs.fa中的序列按长度从小到大排序，写入seqs_sorted.fa文件
seqs_sorted=sorted(seqs_dict.values(), key=lambda x:len(x[1]))
f_seqs_sorted=open("data/seqs_sorted.fa", "wt")
for item in seqs_sorted:
    f_seqs_sorted.write(item[0]+"\n"+item[1]+"\n")
f_seqs_sorted.close()

# 将seqs.fa中的核酸序列转为单行，存入seqs_single_line.fa文件
f_seqs_single=open("data/seqs_single_line.fa", "wt")
for key in seqs_dict.keys():
    f_seqs_single.write(seqs_dict[key][0]+"\n"+seqs_dict[key][1]+"\n")
f_seqs_single.close()

# 将seqs.fa中的核酸序列转为多行，每行长度固定为80个字符，存为seqs_multi_line.fa文件
f_seqs_multi=open("data/seqs_multi_line.fa", "wt")
for item in seqs_dict.values():
    f_seqs_multi.write(item[0]+"\n")
    for i in range(0,len(item[1]),80):
        f_seqs_multi.write(item[1][i:(len(item[1]) if (i+80>len(item[1])) else i+80)]+"\n")
f_seqs_multi.close()
There are 1294 sequences in the FASTA file.

5.7 作业：FATSQ文件处理

  • 读取reads.fastq
  • 统计reads.fastq中的序列数
  • 提取ID为reads_id_list.txt中ID的reads在reads.fastq中的序列，存入f_selected_seqs文件中
  • 计算reads.fastq中的reads长度

关于这部分请参阅20180121_02_CT_Python_training-chinese2.ipynb

fin=open("data/reads.fastq", "rt")

seqs_dict={}
seq_id=""
annotation=""
sequence=""
i=0
for line in fin:
    if i%4==0:
        sp=line.strip().split(" ")
        seq_id=sp[0][1:]
        annotation=line.strip()
    elif i%4==1:
        sequence=line.strip()
        if not seq_id in seqs_dict:
            seqs_dict[seq_id]=[annotation,sequence]
    i=i+1

fin.close()

# 统计reads.fastq中的序列数
sequence_count=len(seqs_dict)
print("There are ", sequence_count, " sequences in the FASTQ file.", sep="")

# 提取ID为reads_id_list.txt中ID的reads在reads.fastq中的序列，存入f_selected_seqs文件中
f_id_list=open("data/reads_id_list.txt", "rt")
f_selected_reads=open("data/selected_reads.fa", "wt")
for line in f_id_list:
    seq_id=line.strip()
    f_selected_reads.write(seqs_dict[seq_id][0]+"\n"+seqs_dict[seq_id][1]+"\n")
f_id_list.close()
f_selected_reads.close()

# 计算reads.fastq中的reads长度
print("The read length in the FASTQ file is ", len(seqs_dict[seq_id][1]), " bp.", sep="")
There are 23993 sequences in the FASTQ file.
The read length in the FASTQ file is 100 bp.

5.8 JSON文件解析

'''
JSON文件是列表和字典的嵌套组合，样式如下
{
    "Speakers": ["Wang Xuning", "MaYingke", "XuKai", "ChenTong"], 
    "Position": "西城区旧鼓楼大街47号院", 
    "Time": "20180120-20180128", 
}

也可以嵌套的更多的层。这种数据结构对存储存在缺失的数据会节省很多空间，
而且每层数据有对应的名字，可以完成批量提取。
'''

import json
fin = open("data/test.json")
jsonD = json.load(fin)
for key,value in list(jsonD.items()):
    print(key,value)
Speakers ['Wang Xuning', 'MaYingke', 'XuKai', 'ChenTong']
Position 西城区旧鼓楼大街47号院
Time 20180120-20180128
# 提取所有speakers
jsonD['Speakers']
['Wang Xuning', 'MaYingke', 'XuKai', 'ChenTong']
  • 把all_species.json转换成一个Python对象，输出所有物种的名字的列表
  • 找出人的乳糖酶基因LCT在马基因组中的同源基因
import requests
import json

ensembl_server="http://rest.ensembl.org"
# 工具函数，发送一个web请求
def do_request(server, service, *args, **kwargs):
    url_params=""
    for a in args:
        if a is not None:
            url_params += "/"+a
    req=requests.get("%s/%s%s" % (server, service, url_params), params=kwargs, headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"})
    if not req.ok:
        req.raise_for_status()
    return req.json

# 通过web请求，得到一个Python对象，含有ensembl服务器上所有物种的信息
all_species=do_request(ensembl_server, "info/species")()

# 把Python对象转换成JSON字符串，写入文件中
fout=open("data/all_species.json", "wt")
print(json.dumps(all_species), file=fout, sep="", end="")
fout.close()

# 从文件中读取JSON字符串，转换为Python对象，输出ensembl服务器上所有物种名
fin=open("data/all_species.json", "rt")
json_line=fin.readline()
all_species=json.loads(json_line)
for sp in all_species["species"]:
    print(sp["name"])

5.9 GenBank文件解析，提取CDS序列

from Bio import SeqIO

with open("data/rna_part.gbk", "r") as input_handle:
    for record in SeqIO.parse(input_handle, "genbank"):
        print(record.id)
        if record.features:
            for feature in record.features:
                if feature.type == "CDS":
                    print(feature.location)
                    print(feature.qualifiers["protein_id"])
                    print(feature.location.extract(record).seq)
